 The Government of India adopted the Constitution of India on 26 November 1949, 70 years before today
 jise 26 janvari 1950 ko lagu kiya gaya tha
 Baba Saheb Dr
 bhimrao ambedkar ko bharat kaa samvidhan nirmaataa kaha jaataa he
 He was the chairman of the Constitution Drafting Committee and it took him 2 years 11 months and 17 days to prepare the final draft of the constitution
 puure desh main 26 november ko samvidhan diwas ke taur par manaaya jaataa he
 Know how important constitution is for the common citizen of India
 samvidhan kii khaas baat ye he ki adhikaar or kartavya yani 'rights and Duites' ke bare main vistaar se varnan kiya gaya he
 Members of the Constituent Assembly were elected by the elected members of the Assemblies of the States of India
 jawaharlal neher, dow
 Bhimrao Ambedkar, Dr
 rajendra prasad, sardaar vallabh bhai patel, moulana abul kalam aaazaad aadi is sabha ke pramukh sadsy the
 Our Constitution is the longest written constitution in the world
 masauda likhane vaali samiti ne samvidhan hindi, angreji main haath se likhakar kallingraph kiya tha or isamen koi typing yaa printing shaamil nahin thi
 Let me tell you, soon after the implementation of the Constitution, the society got a fair justice system
 nagarikon ko moulik adhikaron kii aazaadee mili or kartavyon kii jimmedaari bhi
 Indian constitution includes these important things- It is written and detailed- Fundamental rights are provided- Freedom of judiciary, freedom of travel, living, speech, religion, education etc
, - Single nationality, - Indian constitution is flexible and non- Both are flexible - abolition of caste system at the national level - Uniform civil code and official languages - The center is similar to a Buddhist 'republic'
 - buddha or buddha anushthan kaa prabhaav- bhartiya samvidhan adhinium main aane ke baad, bharat main mahilaon ko matdaan kaa adhikaar mila he
 - Various countries around the world have adopted the Indian Constitution
 ambedkar ko kiya jaataa he yadbhaarat main rashtriya samvidhan diwas 26 november ko har saal sarkari taur par manaaya jaataa he
 The father of this constitution, Dr
 bhimrao raamji ambedkar ko yaad kiya he

 unka maananaa tha ki vibhinn virgon ke bich antar ko baraabar karnaa mahatvapurn tha, anyathaa desh kii ekta ko banaae rakhana bahut mushkil hoga
 He emphasized religious, gender and caste equality

to download Mi Apps shaomi smartphone main me pe ap ko downlod karne ke liye sabase pehle aapako me apstore (mi App Store) main janaa hoga

 If you do not have a me account, you can also create

 This has happened, now let's talk about the first option
 doosraa opshan he- send tu bank acount (send To Bank Account)
